Special Telecommunications Supplement

Respectful Announcement to Overseas Representatives of the Fifth National Congress from the International Radio Station

— Zhen

The Fifth National Congress, which has attracted worldwide attention, opened in Nanjing on the 12th of this month. The representatives, as the backbone of the Party, have come from afar with the sincere intention of uniting to overcome national difficulties. Their presence at the Congress, with their grand plans and wise discussions, will surely fulfill our hopes. Among the Congress representatives are 90 overseas representatives, who are concerned about the perilous state of the motherland and are making inspections of their homeland. Their significance is particularly important and great. Since the outbreak of national crisis, various construction projects in the country have made considerable achievements. If the representatives were to make a casual inspection, they would know the details. In the realm of telecommunications, we at the International Radio Station would like to briefly explain the international telecommunications business, which is closely related to overseas Chinese.

For the past 50 years, our country's international telecommunications business has been managed by foreign underwater cable companies. Not only has there been a huge loss of telegraph fees flowing overseas every year, but our sovereignty has also been undermined. The control of communication between overseas Chinese and our countrymen, in particular, has been a political and economic detriment. It was not until the government established itself in the north and south in the 17th year of the Republic of China, creating a new nation, that it sought to safeguard the independence of our external communications sovereignty. Thus, the Ministry of Communications built the National International Radio Station in Shanghai. After eight years of effort, the following direct communication circuits were established: (1) China-America route: Direct communication with the American Radio Corporation in San Francisco, with the latter's radio station and Western Union Telegraph Company relaying telegrams to various places in North and South America.

(2) China-America route: Direct communication with the Mackay Company's radio station in San Francisco, with the latter's radio station and the Postal Telegraph Company relaying telegrams to various places in North and South America.

(3) China-Germany route: Direct communication with the German Postal and Telegraph Department's radio station in Berlin, directly reaching various places in Germany, and relaying telegrams to various places in Europe and Africa.

(4) China-France route: Direct communication with the French Radio Corporation's radio station in Paris, directly reaching various places in France, and relaying telegrams to various places in Europe and Africa.

(5) China-Russia route: Direct communication with the Soviet Russian Transportation Committee's radio station in Moscow, directly reaching various places throughout Russia.

(6) China-Switzerland route: Direct communication with the Swiss Radio Corporation's radio station in Geneva, directly reaching various places throughout Switzerland.

(7) China-England route: Direct communication with the Royal Traffic Corporation's radio station in London, directly reaching various places throughout England, and relaying telegrams to various countries in Europe and British Africa, India, and Australia.

(8) China-Philippines route: Direct communication with the American Radio Corporation's radio station in Manila, directly reaching various places throughout the Philippines, and relaying telegrams to the Americas and Siam.

(9) China-Vietnam route: Direct communication with the Saigon Vietnam Postal and Telegraph General Bureau's radio station, directly reaching various places throughout Vietnam.

(10) China-Netherlands route: Direct communication with the Dutch East Indies Radio Station in Batavia, directly reaching various places throughout Java, and relaying telegrams to the Netherlands, Australia, India, and Southeast Asia.

(11) China-Japan route: Direct communication with the Radio Telegraph Company's radio station in Tokyo, directly reaching various places throughout Japan.

(12) Shanghai-Hong Kong route: Direct communication with the Hong Kong Postal General Bureau's radio station.

(13) China-Italy route: Direct communication with Italy's Rome Radio Station, directly reaching various places in Italy.

The author has taken the trouble to list the above circuits and explain the places that can be directly reached because the representatives are living abroad and may not know or fully understand the country's telecommunications business and its circuits. If the information is clarified, we know that the representatives are very concerned about the country and will, after returning, advise Chinese people in all regions that all telegrams sent to the country must have "Via Radio Via Anten" (via International Station) marked in the remarks section at the bottom of each telegram, which is a symbol of love for the country.

Furthermore, in the past eight years, all the staff of the International Radio Station have worked hard, and have achieved the highest records in the speed and accuracy of transmitting telegrams. For example, the highest speed for telegrams sent from Shanghai to New York is only four minutes, and the highest speed for telegrams sent from Shanghai to Hong Kong and Manila is only one or two minutes. Furthermore, errors are extremely rare. According to statistics, the total number of incoming and outgoing telegrams at the station in 1933, after complaints from recipients, showed that only 1.27 percent of the errors were due to the station's fault. The International Radio Station operates so efficiently that, through the efforts of the various bureaus and stations to attract customers, the business has grown daily. The number of incoming and outgoing words was 2,922,268 in 1931, increased to 3,650,674 in 1932, and increased to 4,028,460 in 1933. In 1934, due to the opening of the China-England and China-Japan routes, the business showed an even greater surge than in previous years. The number of telegrams reached 50,000 per month, with more than 7 million words, gradually matching the foreign underwater cable companies that have been in business for decades.

Since the establishment of the International Radio Station, our country's international communications have been able to restore freedom. In other words, the relationship between overseas Chinese and the motherland has been strengthened and tightened. Today, the motherland is seeking assistance from Chinese people overseas for various construction projects. It is hoped that the overseas representatives will convey the achievements of the International Radio Station's construction to Chinese people in various places so that they understand the content of the station and know what to choose when sending telegrams. If this happens, it will be a great fortune. As for the magnificence of the station's architecture, the novelty of its machinery, and the thoughtfulness of its services, the station will be happy to provide the representatives with a sincere reception if they visit Shanghai and come to see it.

Nanjing Telegraph Office Gifts Overseas Representatives of the Fifth National Congress Commemorative Cups

Supporting the New Currency System

— Ming

Like a thunderclap, the new currency system policy was officially implemented by the Ministry of Finance starting from the 4th of this month! Regarding the implementation of the new currency system policy, its benefits for our nation's economic future and the various reasons for its implementation have already been clearly explained by the financial authorities and economic experts, so this publication need not elaborate further. In short, this policy, if implemented effectively, is the most perfect method for the revival of our nation's economy.

As for our telecommunications sector, we have a few other thoughts regarding the realization of this new policy: Firstly, what we have always felt was inconvenient is that the currency terms were too complex. Not to mention coins, even paper money often had dozens of varieties in one place, making it difficult to remember and distinguish. Sometimes, even though the bank that issued the paper money had already collapsed, the paper money had not disappeared from the market. Sometimes, even though a bank was in operation, doubts arose about the banknotes it issued because the bank was not very well-known. Therefore, the telecommunications bureau and the public often encountered many unnecessary disputes when making payments or collecting telegram fees. As for using coins, many misunderstandings often occurred due to the varying fineness and the mixture of genuine and counterfeit coins. Now that the use of coins has been prohibited, and only the banknotes of the Central Bank of China, the Bank of China, and the Bank of Communications are stipulated as legal tender, other bank notes are permitted to circulate temporarily, but must be gradually exchanged. In the near future, the various miscellaneous currencies on the market will be eliminated, and only the banknotes of the three major banks will circulate. Disputes between the telecommunications bureau and the public due to currency will inevitably be reduced to a minimum, or even eliminated.

Secondly, in the past, the minting of coins was mostly done freely by the provinces due to their independent governance. As a result, the fineness was low and did not meet the legal standard. For example, the "hao yang" circulating in the Pearl River basin and the "chuan yang" circulating in Sichuan province could not be fully used due to insufficient fineness. The former required a discount when used and could not be valued according to the face value. Moreover, the currency price varied from morning to evening, making it difficult for the telecommunications bureau to convert the "taiyang" to calculate the telegram fee. Sometimes, the price fluctuation was too great within a single day, resulting in considerable losses. The latter could be fully used within Sichuan province, but when exchanged outside the province, a premium of 40% or more was sometimes required, while various telecommunications machinery and materials had to be purchased with full silver dollars. Therefore, the telecommunications business income within Sichuan province was effectively reduced by 40%. These situations had a very large impact on the telecommunications economic policy, enough to hinder the development of the telecommunications industry. Now that legal tender has been implemented, various miscellaneous currencies must be gradually withdrawn, without a doubt. Soon, the currency price across the country will be unified, and there will be no difference in high and low prices. The telecommunications revenue will naturally not suffer this loss again.

Thirdly, in addition, we feel a common difficulty, which is giving change. Because the value of various currencies is not fixed and changes frequently, the telecommunications bureau's business offices must post the silver currency exchange rate daily. At the same time, because the legally defined "li", "fen", and "jiao" decimal fractional currencies have not been officially minted and issued, it is difficult to accurately find and exchange the correct amount. Therefore, there is always some loss on one side between the sender and the telegraph office. Therefore, several telecommunications bureaus, in order to avoid losses for both parties and for the convenience of handling matters, mostly use postage stamps for change. However, once the postage stamps are stained, they are difficult to use. Therefore, this method is not welcomed by every telegrapher. Therefore, the fundamental solution still lies in the rapid minting of legally defined standard fractional currency. It is heard that the financial authorities have ordered the mint to start minting 5-li, 1-fen, 2.5-fen, and 5-fen copper coins, as well as 1-jiao, 2-jiao, and 5-jiao nickel coins, in order to thoroughly implement the new currency system policy. In the future, these legal fractional currencies will be used in the market, and all illegal standard copper and silver miscellaneous currencies currently circulating in the market will be gradually withdrawn. We hope that the Ministry of Finance will implement this method as soon as possible, so that the telecommunications agencies will no longer have to post the silver currency exchange rate, and at the same time reduce all unnecessary troubles.

Therefore, all of us in the telecommunications sector should absolutely support the implementation of the new currency system policy.

(5) Our country's telecommunications policy is currently striving to improve

In recent years, our country's transportation authorities have indeed changed a lot in terms of telecommunications policy. For example, the merger of wireless telecommunications, the joint establishment of telecommunications and postal offices, the installation of new-style Catter telecommunications machines, and other new facilities are all sufficient to increase the speed of telegram transmission and provide the public with full convenience. The reporter deeply believes that as national affairs gradually become stable and various industries develop equally, the social need for telegrams will increase, and telecommunications equipment will become more complete. Conversely, if the people do not need telegrams and the bureau's business cannot develop, then even if the transportation authorities strive to improve, it will be laborious and useless, and will not achieve the goal of benefiting the country and the people.

The world often believes that our country's telegram rates are too high and cannot be popularized among the people. This saying may have some merit. However, after the telegram rates are reduced, the people's desire to send telegrams may still not increase. If income decreases on one hand and telegram business does not increase on the other, then a major financial problem will arise, and it will be even more difficult to sustain. What is currently hoped for is the development of domestic transportation and the advancement of various industries, first creating a dynamic and lively society to increase the driving force for sending telegrams. Secondly, the people's habit of using telegrams must also be gradually cultivated. In this way, with all parties advancing in parallel and taking both facts into account, I believe the transportation authorities will be able to carefully consider the situation, plan comprehensively, and find ways to reduce the telegram rates to seek further popularization.

(5) Hoping for cooperation from all parties

Telegram communication has a great relationship with the country and the people. In foreign countries, whether it is commercially operated or government-run, the people do their best to maintain and supervise it in good faith. The current state of telegrams in our country, in terms of management equipment and machinery, may not be as perfect and sophisticated as in foreign countries, but it has generally taken shape. If given time and a good environment, improving equipment and adding new machines will not be difficult to catch up with foreign countries. Therefore, it is deeply hoped that all sectors of the country will cooperate and assist in good faith. The development of the telegram business can directly promote the advancement of various industries, and indirectly raise the status of the country and the nation. As for facilitating public communication and connecting the feelings of all sectors, its relationship is still considered small.

September 22nd, Republic of China, in London, England

The State of Telegrams in Countries Like England and the United States and the Reasons for Their Development (Continued)

— Li Jiqing

(3) The Reasons for the Development of Telegrams in Countries Like England and the United States

The telegram business in countries like England and the United States is indeed very developed, but there are various reasons why it is so developed. The reporter traveled to various places and observed in detail, and learned that there are many reasons. A few are summarized as follows:

(1) Convenient Transportation The transportation in countries like England and the United States is extremely convenient. There are airplanes in the air, trains on land, and ships on the water. In addition, the roads are well-connected in all directions, and cars come and go like weaving. Therefore, the people and all things in society are constantly active day and night. As a result of this activity, the social situation and personal interactions have become unusually complex, and the telegrams that transmit news have increased greatly. Our country has few railways, and even fewer highways. The aviation industry has not yet become widespread, and sea and river transportation is also developing. Therefore, the people in various places have lived in one place for a long time, and rarely travel far unless there is an urgent matter. Life is extremely quiet, and personal interactions tend to be simple. The transmission of news has no time sensitivity, and the need for telegrams is not significant. In recent years, the number of domestic railways has increased, highways have developed, and the degree of social activity has gradually increased. The need for telegrams will inevitably increase. This is indeed a good phenomenon.

(2) Prosperous Industry and Commerce In various places in the United States and England, there are large-scale factories manufacturing various daily necessities. The scope of their commercial operations mostly extends to all parts of the world. With the development of industry and commerce, matters such as promoting sales orders and transportation negotiations must rely on the convenience of telegrams to seek speed and profit. Telegram exchanges have increased as a result, and various telecommunications companies are working day and night to strive for rapid transmission.

(3) People Can Utilize The people of the United States and England are very good at utilizing telegrams. In addition to handling legitimate matters and of course sending telegrams to transmit news, they also make extensive use of telegrams for travel entertainment and ordinary social affairs. When traveling, they send telegrams to inform family and friends of their departure and arrival. For weddings, funerals, and celebrations, they send telegrams to express congratulations and condolences. During festivals, they send telegrams to congratulate each other. In addition, people related to various gatherings and theatrical performances also express their feelings through telegrams. Their use of telegrams can truly be said to be meticulous. Compared to the situation in our country where telegrams are not sent unless there is an important matter, and people feel panicked when they see telegrams, it is a big difference. The fact that people in countries like England and the United States are good at using telegrams is not only because telegram rates are not expensive, but also because they have a habit of sending telegrams. As for their telegram rates, the reporter carefully studied and felt that compared to their monthly salary, it is not cheaper than in our country. Our country's current rate for social telegrams seems extremely low, equivalent to just over one dime in US dollars, and about seven pence in British currency, which is actually similar to the prices in England and the United States.

(4) Simple Characters The development of telegrams in countries like England and the United States owes much to the simplicity of the characters. The characters in countries like England, the United States, Germany, and France all evolved from more than twenty letters. What can be said can be written, and the application is extremely convenient. Moreover, the modern method of transmitting telegrams all uses typewriter-style receiving and sending machines. The telegram is sent on the machine at location A using the typewriter method, and the same telegram is received on the typewriter-style machine at location B, which can be read. Sometimes, the sender can even use this machine to send telegrams themselves and deal directly with the receiver without going through the telegram bureau's agency. It seems that our people cannot enjoy this kind of convenience, because the characters are complex and there are many dialects. The telegram must first be translated into numbers and then translated into the telegram text. Such complicated procedures are inconvenient for both the sender and receiver, and cause various difficulties for the telecommunications bureau. Our country's telecommunications bureau is now equipped with the same new-style telecommunications machines as the telecommunications companies in England and the United States, but because our country's characters are not as simple as theirs, it seems that we cannot achieve the highest effectiveness. The Ministry of Transportation is currently sending personnel to study the Mandarin telegram method. In the future, after its implementation, it will definitely provide great convenience to the public in sending and receiving telegrams. Reading domestic newspapers overseas, I learned that the Ministry of Education is currently promoting the simplified character method, and there is a movement to simplify characters in the country, which is truly gratifying. The slow progress of our country's various undertakings is also greatly caused by the complexity of the characters and dialects. The inability of telegram handling to be sufficiently quick has a significant relationship with this matter.

(5) Our Redundant Official Military Telegrams

The various commercially operated telecommunications companies in the United States and the government-run postal and telecommunications administration in England all charge fees according to regulations for each telegram: half price for official telegrams and full fee for commercial telegrams. There is no situation where sending and receiving a telegram provides an income, but official telegrams are recorded without payment, or only material costs are charged. Official telegrams, whether in plain language or code, are quite concise, with very few empty words. Our country's official military telegrams, on the other hand, often contain parallel prose, polite greetings, or involve private matters. Sometimes they are sent to all parts of the country, widely distributed to unnecessary agencies, and the words "extremely urgent" are added before the telegram, limiting it to "immediate arrival". This kind of situation, added at will by the secretary at a moment of pleasure, causes congestion of the lines, hinders commercial telegrams, and increases procedures for the telecommunications bureau, which is extremely disadvantageous. This is something that telecommunications personnel handling telecommunications affairs in foreign countries would never dream of. If a telecommunications company in England and the United States has telegrams, it has income. With income, it can strive for development. The development of its telecommunications business is based on this reason.

All Sorts of Misunderstandings Caused by Users Due to Connection

— Ye Linsheng's Speech

This article is what Mr. Ye spoke at Guangpantai, Wuxian. Regarding users various misunderstandings, said reasonably. This journal is happy to publish it. All people who make use of telephone, please find time to read it, it is hoped! Editor's note

Fellow users, and people who are telephone users: Today I come to report an important piece of telecommunications common sense. That is when you use the telephone at times, and feel that it is inconvenient – especially in moldy weather, in your opinions, maybe you think it is the telephone bureau's operator personnel who gave up on their duties, and makes things difficult for the user. This kind of thing can be said cannot be completely impossible. Also, cannot say the operator must have no fault. However, you must know, the telephone bureau's operators – that is, the connecting personnel – they are under the strict supervision of the leaders and the chiefs at all times. If they deliberately violate regulations and commit other things, they will certainly receive severe punishment, and will definitely not be forgiven. Therefore, the words "deliberately making things difficult for the user," I am afraid that while theory has this, it will not exist in reality. According to statistics, of all the reports regarding user inquiries, eight or nine out of ten originate from misunderstandings on both sides. Therefore, there is a need to explain these misunderstandings. In other words, there is a need to make you users understand the reasons for the misunderstandings.

Now I will report the various obstacles, as well as the reasons why users have misunderstandings, using the method of analysis, to make it clear.

First type The reason why the bureau cannot answer

(1) Two lines are connected or interrupted;

(2) User's telephone has an obstacle, or the bureau's switchboard has a problem, causing the light not to light up.

"Note" Shared-line switchboard, each user has a light.

You must know, when calling a telephone, the bureau does not come to answer, it is no more than these problems, not the operator deliberately ignoring it. You should notify the telephone bureau via a nearby telephone or letter, so that they can send a craftsman to repair it at any time.

Second type The reason for slow response

(1) Shared-line exchange switchboard, each operator manages an average of more than 240 households. There are often more than ten households that want to dial at the same time. Operators cannot answer at the same time. They have to answer in order, so it is inevitable that it will take a little longer to answer the last household!

Third type Wrong number and name

(1) Different accents in different places, the operator mishears. Sounds like 1742 are most easily misheard.

(2) Users do not look at the number book, and the number correction slip that is sent every month. The number reported has already been changed to another house. The operator connects according to the number reported, but the user thinks the connection is wrong.

Fourth type Interrupted call

(1) When the user is speaking, the cord on the switchboard suddenly has a problem, or some street lines are suddenly broken or touched by the wind. In this case, the conversation will of course be interrupted.

Although the user has finished calling the number, but the one who was called has not come, or the person being looked for has not come, it stands to reason that the receiver cannot be hung up. If at this time, one party hangs up the receiver, hanging up the receiver is the signal that the call has ended. The operator sees that the user has already indicated that the call has ended, and will naturally disconnect the user. At this time, the other user who is speaking will definitely suspect that the operator is causing trouble, but who knows that the operator is taking the blame for someone else?

(3) If the user has a sub-machine installed, when the sub-machine is in a call, and the main machine also wants to make a call at the same time, if you are not careful and flip the switch over, then the person speaking on the sub-machine will not be able to hear the end of the conversation. Fifth type The user calls but does not come or answers slowly

(1) The line has an obstacle, the ringing current cannot pass through, and the bell will not ring.

(2) Most users telephones do not have a dedicated person guarding them. Sometimes the owner goes out and locks the door of the telephone room, then even if the bell rings, no one will answer.

Sixth type Various other misunderstandings

(1) During the conversation between the two users, one party occasionally does not answer, mistaking it for the bureau having disconnected the line!

(2) The party being called hears the bell ringing, picks up the receiver without speaking, and at this time suddenly talks and laughs with someone, or someone nearby scolds, and the party wanting the number hears it, thinking that the operator is scolding people.

(3) The party being called has a line obstacle, and the bureau replies "line is bad". At this time, the damaged user has just repaired it, or is blown open by the wind at this time. The party wanting the number learns of it, and is certain to suspect that the operator is causing trouble.

(4) The number that the user wants is often unable to be connected immediately because it is talking with another household. The user thinks that the operator is intentionally perfunctory, unaware that the busier the exchange is, the more users are talking and unable to be connected, not that the operator is intentionally perfunctory. Because each operator connects a line without any effort, if they perfunctorily answer users with words such as "someone is calling" or "the line is busy", the user is bound to ask for the number again. Resulting in having to connect eventually, wouldn't this be more troublesome the more perfunctory it is?

In short: In the future, if there is any inconvenience in connecting, you can notify the telephone bureau separately, and the telephone bureau will definitely accept it sincerely, find out the truth, and give a satisfactory answer. However, before the facts are clear, you must not arbitrarily assume that "this is the operator causing trouble" or "a certain telephone bureau is bad", because before the facts have been clarified and resolved, the conclusion reached is the user's one-sided suspicion and misunderstanding. What is needed between the telephone bureau and the users now is sincere cooperation, and there must be no suspicion and misunderstanding. Once there is a misunderstanding, it will affect the development of the national telecommunications industry!

Discussing the Standard Writing of Telegrams

— Wang Hengyun

Regarding the writing method of telegrams, there is originally no limit to the format. The main condition is "clarity". However, if you can write in a more standard way, it will increase the speed of telegrams and help the telecommunications bureau staff a lot. The standard format for writing telegrams is very simple and easy to do. It is a win-win method that is convenient for yourself and suitable for others. I think the people who send telegrams must be very happy to do it.

The text used to send telegrams is divided into two types: one is foreign language telegrams, and the other is Chinese telegrams. For foreign language telegrams, whether in plain code or cipher, as long as they are transcribed clearly, or copied on paper using a typewriter, it can be said to be a very perfect format. Chinese telegrams require more procedures because they must be translated into numbers. Chinese cipher telegrams use four or five numbers as a group, combined according to the cipher book compiled separately by the sender, so they must be translated into numbers and sent by the sender themselves. As for Chinese plain language telegrams, it is stipulated that they must be translated according to the code listed in the newly compiled plain code cipher telegrams published by the Ministry of Transportation, and the meaning of the telegram must be connected into a coherent text. The sender can translate it themselves according to the newly compiled code, or they can just write out the Chinese characters and ask the telegraph office to translate it for them. However, for this kind of self-translated plain code telegram, the original text must be noted next to the code so that the telegraph office's receiving staff can check whether their translation is wrong on behalf of the sender. Because they have the responsibility to correct errors and verify the telegram. Regarding this kind of self-translated plain code telegram, some people think that noting the original telegram text is an extra procedure. In reality, it is not. Because anyway, when sending a telegram, you always have to write out the telegram draft first before you can translate it. Then, write the telegram draft more loosely and translate the code below each character. Wouldn't it be more convenient? And it guarantees that there are absolutely no errors in the translation of this telegram.

For the paper used to write telegrams, the telegraph office has prepared very exquisite and suitable telegram paper, with the telegram format and telegram regulations printed on it. Anyone who sends telegrams can go to various telegraph offices or telegram receiving and sending offices to ask for it, free of charge. If you don't use the paper issued by the telegraph office, you can do whatever you want, but it is best to write horizontally from left to right. This is the custom for writing telegrams. If the telegram is written horizontally from left to right according to this custom, the telegraph office staff can send it out without hesitation, which will greatly increase the speed of your telegram. On the other hand, if the telegram is written from right to left or vertically from top to bottom, then it is not very standard. Although it can still be sent and received in the same way and will not be delayed, the staff cannot help but read it, because this writing method is not the customary order. Therefore, when writing telegrams, write horizontally from left to right. This is the standard way of writing.

A Guarantee for Sending Money Order Telegrams

— Baozhen

Banks established by countries or private individuals in Europe and America, in order to prevent evil people from using the name to send fake telegrams with the intention of deceiving money for profit, mostly agree on a secret code check word or check number in advance. The bank sending the telegram writes it before the text of the money order telegram. After receiving the telegram, the bank receiving the telegram must verify the secret code check word or check number used before the incoming telegram to avoid being counterfeited and defrauded of money. This method is very good. The international telegram rules also stipulate that "bank telegrams and similar telegrams, if the text contains a secret code check word or check number, are still considered plain language telegrams." Our country's telegraph office has always allowed the use of secret code check words or check numbers for foreign language plain language telegrams sent by domestic or foreign banks. However, there is no such stipulation for Chinese plain language telegrams. It was not until August of the 23rd year that the various telegraph offices received an order from the Ministry of Transportation stipulating that, starting from September 1st of the 23rd year, the text of Chinese plain language money order telegrams sent by banks or money changers should also be allowed to use a secret code check word and an Arabic numeral indicating the date and number of the telegram at the beginning or end to prevent counterfeiting. All of these check words, numbers, and other words in the text will still be charged according to the Chinese plain language telegram rates. It is heard that this stipulation has already been published in the current domestic telegram business rules and is used as a fixed rule.

The majority of those who send money order telegrams are banks or money changers, but other merchants who have commercial money exchanges with merchants in other places also often need to use telegrams for quick remittance. For example, "Hankou Minsheng Road Yapu Electric Company – Pay Chang Zhuang (500) yuan, Central Bank (7200) yuan, Main Factory Foundry", its nature is no different from a money order telegram. Regarding the large amount of money in and out, it is also especially necessary to add the above-mentioned secret code check word. It is learned that the Ministry of Transportation has also allowed various merchants to send Chinese plain language telegrams for the purpose of remittance to follow the example of bank and money changer telegrams and use a secret code check word and an Arabic numeral indicating the date and number of the telegram at the beginning or end of the text. From now on, various merchants can get a reliable guarantee when sending money order telegrams. As for money order telegrams sent by individuals, the sender and receiver can agree on a word in advance to be used as the sender's signature, and its function can be comparable to a secret code check word. The telegraph office has no restrictions on the word used for the sender's signature, and the sender can choose any word.

Next, regarding the writing method of secret code check words and date numbers, I will briefly describe it as follows. According to the regulations in Section 3 of Article 20 of Chapter 6 of the International Telegraph Rules and Section G of Article 6 of the Foreign Language Telegram Writing and Charging Method, the number of letters or numbers contained in the check word or check number in a foreign language plain language telegram is limited to a maximum of five. As for the secret code check word in a Chinese plain language telegram, it is limited to four codes, such as (9717). Also, according to the regulations in Section B of Article 54 of the current domestic telegram business rules, the above-mentioned check word and date number must be written in parentheses (the parentheses symbol is free of charge) and a "number" character must be added after each. However, if there are no other characters or numbers in between, only one "number" character needs to be added after the second parenthesis, such as (9717)(1601) number. Therefore, it is not appropriate to write this series of check words and date numbers separately. If they are written consecutively at the beginning or end of the text, one "number" character can be saved, reducing one character's telegram fee. (End)

A Visit to the Ministry of Communications' Telegraph and Telephone Machine Repair and Manufacturing Facility

— Hua

—High-Quality Products, Low Prices—

The Ministry of Communications' Telegraph and Telephone Machine Repair and Manufacturing Facility is the only institution established by the Ministry of Communications to manufacture telegraph and telephone machinery. It is also the only factory in the country that supplies telecommunications machinery. Although its scale and equipment are not particularly grand compared to other machine industries in the country, due to the rapid advancement of internal management and manufacturing technology, its products not only serve the needs of the agencies under the Ministry of Communications, but also telegraph machinery needed by various important railways in the country are vying to order from it. Recently, the reporter had the opportunity to visit the entire factory and dares to briefly describe it to introduce it to readers:

We know that the manufacturing of a piece of machinery involves complex work such as drafting, carpentry, casting, forging, fitting, turning, assembly, and testing. The manufacturing process within the repair and manufacturing facility, except for a portion of the casting work which is contracted out to local foundries, is all handled by the facility itself. What we saw included manufacturing workshops, electroplating workshops, paint spraying workshops, and bakelite workshops. The manufacturing workshop includes (1) carpentry room, (2) fitting room, (3) lathe room, (4) planing room, (5) drilling room, (6) broaching room, (7) milling room, (8) hardening room, and (9) assembly room. The workers were all busily working. The sound of the machinery was deafening, demonstrating the intensity of the work.

According to Mr. Lin Dongchen, an engineer at the facility, "Although our facility is an affiliated institution of the Ministry of Communications, it is economically self-sufficient. The Ministry of Communications only provided the initial establishment funds! After several years of concerted effort by all personnel, we have now achieved a considerable foundation. However, the facility's funds are still limited, and everything still requires the maintenance and expansion by the authorities. The facility's staff are all graduates from well-known domestic universities and specialized schools in mechanical engineering. Although the compensation is extremely meager due to the facility's funding constraints, their ability to endure hardship and perform tasks is outstanding, which deserves our praise. The facility's management of workers focuses on skill and moral training, ensuring that every worker has good character and excellent skills. The facility has basketball court facilities to provide workers with physical training. Every evening, workers also receive two hours of classes, instructed by the facility's staff. Workers are naturally greatly helped in the facility's production under such good cultivation. In terms of the facility's business over the past two years, the Ministry of Communications is naturally our largest customer, but now a significant portion of the telegraph machinery used by major railways is also supplied by our facility. Although the facility's machinery has increased significantly over the past few years, it is still felt to be insufficient due to business expansion. We are actively expanding to meet actual needs. Mr. Shu Zhendong, the facility's manager, is the inventor of the Shu Shi Chinese typewriter at the Commercial Press. He has a deep foundation and strong interest in machinery. Therefore, although Mr. Shu also serves as the director of the Capital Telephone Bureau and is very busy with official duties, he makes sure to come to the repair and manufacturing facility every afternoon to personally supervise. The facility's current position is naturally due to the assistance provided by Manager Shu.”

The reporter was extremely satisfied after listening to the above remarks from Engineer Lin and visiting the internal workshops of the repair and manufacturing facility. It is urgent to record this to substantiate this publication.

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Discussion

What is Hoped for in Chinese Women

— Xing An

A-jing telegram: On the 8th, the masses requested the A-huang to reward three women in the Heberley River Basin who assisted their husbands in resisting the Italian army. Two of them crawled for an hour under Italian artillery fire to supply ammunition to the frontline machine gun team, only retreating when ammunition was exhausted. The third woman commanded five soldiers to tenaciously defend the outpost trenches and ensure the safe retreat of the five soldiers.

Women occupy a very important position in today's society. Social work requires women's efforts, political work requires women's participation, and even military work requires women's assistance. This is undeniable in the current extraordinary era.

But what is the situation of women in our country in retrospect? The vast majority of old-fashioned women, needless to say, have become prisoners of feudal forces. Furthermore, they have neither the fortune to receive education nor the opportunity to participate in social work. To say that these women abandon their responsibility to society is more like society rejecting their contributions. As for a portion of new-era women, although they have been influenced by Western ideas, some are willing to be playthings for men, while others still regard being a virtuous wife and good mother as their highest goal. There are also many people who want to drive them back into the kitchen. There are also a few women who claim to be enlightened, but they only focus on fighting for equal rights between men and women. It is very rare to see those who demand to dedicate themselves to society and fulfill their obligations to society.

The new era has already arrived before our eyes, which is an opportunity for women to develop their abilities. Women in A country have already assisted men in resisting the enemy. The environment our country is currently in can be considered extremely difficult. It is hoped that Chinese women in general can also take on a share of the responsibility for saving the country.

The Disappointed Crowd

— Lin Hao

This is a street that can only accommodate two people walking side by side. Outside the street is the pier of Changxing Rice Firm. Open boats from the countryside are moored there haphazardly. The boats are filled with new rice, and the weight is too much, pressing the hulls very low, almost half buried in the water, rooted, without even a ripple. Three or five boatmen squat on the bow or stern, chatting about heaven and earth.

Changxing Rice Firm is on that side of the street. The morning sunlight is faint and weak, shining there, precisely illuminating several big men wearing tattered felt hats, dressed in ragged clothes, and with faces sunburnt to a purplish-brown color. They had just rushed up from the pier, not even catching their breath: "Sir, how's the market?"

"Coarse rice is five and a half, grain is three and a half." Wearing a pair of tortoiseshell glasses, looking very important, he said haughtily, this, it is said, is the accountant of Changxing Rice Firm.

"What?" [Unclear text]

Page 22

cold water, they were surprised. Where did the fiery hope of just now go? Ah! Did it grow wings and fly away? Not believing it, they only felt their own eyes blurring, stopping for so long: "I remember selling it for eleven and a half in June this year, you..."

"June is June, now is now, don't talk nonsense. Why don't you say you bought it for fourteen that year, let alone eleven and a half."

"Oh!..." Feeling that there was nothing to say: "But, sir, how can it fall so fast?"

"That's strange enough. Don't you think about what year it is? People don't even have spare money for food, who can afford to sell it expensive? Besides, rice from everywhere is flooding in like a tide. Judging by the current situation, humph! It will fall even lower in a few days!"

"Then,... sir, please raise the price a bit?" The one wearing the felt hat pleaded.

"Tch!" Not good, the gentleman smiled coldly, with more to say: "Raise the price? Then we'd have to work for nothing. Such a big rice firm, so many employees, everyone would starve to death!"

"Sir, can you save us farmers? Raise it a bit, we're so pitiful!"

"Sir, please have some kindness! The price is really too pitifully low, please add some?"

"The same as last year, eight yuan and two? We'll just have to ask you to earn a little less, sir..."

"Look, how long-winded these people are," the accountant said to another gentleman, pointing his finger at this group wearing felt hats, then turning his head back: "If none of you think the price is high enough, then don't sell it! You have goods and we have money, we don't interfere with each other, what's the point of being long-winded? Aren't there two more boats coming over there?" Pointing to the pier, showing off extremely, turning his head with the tortoiseshell glasses away.

Everyone was like a lamb to be slaughtered, privately turning to the stone steps to discuss:

"I think we should row to Liu Village?"

"That's not right, it's said that they've had a meeting among themselves, I'm afraid they won't go up or down?"

"Hmph... Do you believe their lies?"

"It's not worth mentioning a meeting among themselves, but rowing there would add another expense for the boat, and it would be the same as Changxing, then we'd be really out of luck! Let's not go to Liu Village!"

"Don't sell it, turn back and take it home!" The indignant one said heavily.

"Hmph! We won't necessarily die if we don't sell it." The gentleman turned his head: "What are those foreign ocean ships bringing in? Really... Tch..." Another cold laugh.

Fiery hope, Changxing Rice Firm, eleven and a half, eight and two, five and a half, foreign ocean ships... Everything seemed to give them a jolt.

The ones who had just docked came again, three or five dark-skinned guys wearing tattered felt hats.

"Ask them, what's the price?"

"Coarse rice is five and a half, grain is three and a half." The gentleman said the same thing.

The fiery hope was shattered, like soap bubbles, another three or five burst.

The first ones looked at the later ones, the later ones looked at the first ones, everyone's stomach felt infinitely empty, and their minds were filled with disappointment. Their eyes shot down to the stone steps, silent like dead water in an ancient well, never to ripple again.

Everyone had a helpless look on their faces.

Thus, the transaction was completed in helplessness. Although they were unwilling to send those snow-white rice grains into Changxing Rice Firm, they needed snow-white silver dollars even more. What they regretted was exchanging those large bags of rice for a small number of silver dollars, and those were green and patterned paper bills:

"Sir, can you exchange them for Yuan Shikai's?"

"Paper money can also be exchanged for things, how stupid! You country bumpkin!"

"Then, please give us the Bank of China's?"

"Hmph! You don't even want the very strong and unbroken Central Bank, do you want... you're preparing to sit on the...?" The gentleman flared up, slapping the counter. He said proudly. The one wearing the felt hat had nothing to say, hanging his head, and went back dejectedly.

In this way, the fervent hopes they had before arriving at this street were destroyed: the wife's fancy clothes, the children's toys, and everything needed... Now, there was nothing left. What they got was not even enough to pay the landlord. They had worked hard for a year in vain. They felt that the world was collapsing, and they felt infinite pain!

The sun reached the top of the head, illuminating this group of disappointed people, gradually moving to the other side of the pier.

Night Inn

— Tian

Four or five points of light scattered in the grass huts surrounded by the mountains, mixed with the flickering fireflies, poured out the lonely night moon, clear as a mirror, from the depths of the valley in the eastern mountains.

The lonely night moon slowly stepped onto the lush treetops, and people on a long journey also hurried. A staggering heart did not shorten the length of the road, and the eerie terror of the clustered ridges appeared after the daytime difficulties. Pulling the steps tighter, thousands of pounds of weight tripped the calves.

—Inn! Inn! Is it so vague!

Fine stones pricked the heart of the feet like needles, and the thick floating skin also felt excruciating pain. The rugged mountain road, like the rugged life, was a hazy shadow, turning from wide and sloping to a narrow path. The lights of the distant village also disappeared, only the fireflies danced brilliantly, and a new moon shone indifferently in a narrow sky.

His feet were not on the ground, and his heart trembled at the tips of every star. The muscles all over his body shrunk the area they occupied, moving his eyes to the pebble road in front of his feet, and moving his heart to all the details of socializing after he arrived in the ancient city of Chang'an. He wanted to grab work, he had to socialize, walking, walking, but linking socializing and money, he couldn't help but think about the loss of the daytime.

Walking, walking, his mind and body were entirely focused on the daytime matter:

Detective! Grabbed! Slapped twice! Detained for two hours! Fined ten dollars! What to do with only five dollars left!

Cold sweat oozed onto his forehead, was it fear or annoyance? Even he himself didn't know. Following the soft, half-withered thorns, he walked slowly. Occasionally looking up, that gloomy pass flashed behind him, but the fierce,不可這視 evil state still startled him.

Finally, he fell from the crevice between the two peaks onto a flat plain locked by night fog. The lights flickered like blinking fireflies, sparsely scattered in the corners, like children seeing strangers. He also looked around like children seeing strangers. His muscles suddenly relaxed, joyfully like dried-up fish leaping into the sea.

—If there's no inn, I'll have to spend the night by the base of the wall.

Looking towards the place where there was light, the sound of footsteps from the terraced fields reverberated in the deep valley of the opposite mountain. The sound waves immediately became hollow and clear. The sensitive barking of dogs echoed the rhythm of his footsteps. He switched the long bag, which weighed only three or four kilograms but felt like thousands of kilograms, to his left shoulder, breathing out all the pent-up air in his chest.

"Inn for Business Travelers" A long sign, vaguely recognizable under the moonlight, a bamboo-framed pergola, shielding the frost of October, the middle-aged and weak him, only felt a little warmer here. A hall-filled kerosene lamp burned three red torches, and he sat down on that bench with peeling patterns.

The night inn was strangely lonely. Besides an old couple in their fifties or so, there was no one else. The fire in the stove had also gone out. The old man opened his bleary eyes and asked tentatively:

"Guest, are you still rushing on after resting for a while?"

"It's late, I want to stay here, is there a place?"

The old man was a little afraid and a little happy: "There is a place, but..."

The old man didn't finish his sentence, but he didn't pursue it either. Seeing the situation, the old couple were reliable. His stomach rumbled, so:

"Please cook some supper for me, I'm hungry."

The old woman cooked, the old man fetched water to wash his feet. He opened his package, took out his shoes and socks, and tied the only twenty-odd silver dollars to his waist.

After eating dinner, the old man led him to a room with three beds lined up, and told him:

"Be careful! This place was robbed three nights ago, it's a pity they even took our tattered clothes and junk!" The old man still had some lingering fear.

"Is that so?—Three nights ago?"

"Yes—be careful, there's a small door here, if there's any movement at the front door, you can escape from here."

After the old man left, only a little kerosene lamp was left. Besides the bed he was sleeping on, the other two beds didn't even have quilts. Dust and cobwebs adorned the four walls, and some black marks remained on the ten walls.

He dared not sleep, but he had to. Yes, this place was deep in the mountains and forests, it should be easy for bandits to come! What to do? The muscles all over his body ached so much that he couldn't move forward even an inch. He used his package as a pillow, put his hands on the money bag around his waist, anxiously, lingeringly, drowsily fell asleep...

Who was it that grabbed his right arm and threw him from the bed to the ground.

He was bewildered. When did they open the door, when did they sneak into the room where he was sleeping, what happened to that old couple, he didn't know at all. Half of his left body trembled with a burst of numbness before he opened his eyes.

"Where's the money? Take it out quickly!" The face of that big man was covered with a thin layer of coal smoke, but his true face could still be recognized. It was those people who claimed to be inspectors during the day, all five or six of them, with several sabers waving shimmeringly on the ground.

"Masters, I don't have any money. Didn't I give it all to you this morning?"

Peng! A slap landed on the old wound, in exactly the same way.

"Where did you give it to us? Nonsense!" Pulling him up, the silver dollars clattered to the ground. "Don't resist!"

In his desperate struggle, the silver money bag was finally untied by them. He howled and cried: "Innkeeper, help! Help!"

Returning Bird

— Xiao Qi

Like a gray pigeon accustomed to wandering, ah, the heart of a traveler, wandering under the vast sky, trekking on a long journey, feels exceptionally tired.

I flew from the north to the south like a pigeon, but three years only brought me back a chest full of disappointment and aged sighs, and lost the brocade dreams of youth, the brocade of longing. Yes, three years is very short, but I have become another person, as if a defeated straggler retreated from the front line, the vigorous, heroic enthusiasm completely died out, only a broken body and mind remained. I threw myself back into my hometown, my hometown still had lush fruit trees, clear rivers, lovely orange skies, and gentle monsoon winds, gentle sunshine, and gentle air. All the charming scenery. However, I had no interest in appreciating it. My heart was simply a stagnant pond, heavy and silent, unable to stir up even a ripple. With that stagnant pond of a heart, dragging my slow steps, I vaguely trampled the ground of my hometown, in the fields, between the bamboo garden fences, in front of the tomb inscriptions. I could almost remember that I had sat on that stone bed, on that lawn, leisurely browsing the color and illusionary posture of the sunset on the distant suburban mountains, while listening to the cowherd riding on the back of the animal, singing a loud, unrhymed mountain song. I would almost be drunk, unaware of the approaching dusk. Now, I pass by every stone bed, every pile of lawn where I once sat in a daze, and I feel nothing, only knowing that I have lost a joyful heart. And those clusters of bamboo gardens have also become desolate ruins. Looking at the vast fields, it is all a white expanse of water, with only a few wild geese swimming back and forth.

Three years, yes, very short, why did everything change all of a sudden?

My own home, on the walls outside the house, two of the three pomegranate trees had died, and the one that survived seemed so lonely. The stamens bloomed as usual, and the fruits bore as usual, but the old and gentle grandmother who had personally planted the pomegranate trees had been in her grave for two years. The father who loved to eat pomegranate fruit, for the sake of the family's livelihood, went to a distant and foreign land, and still often did not forget to instruct in his letters to cultivate it well, and not let it wither. The pomegranate is a symbol of happiness! These words were also the grandmother's dying words. The sound of the old grandmother telling stories has disappeared, and the talkative voice of the father has been separated, so the home seems very lonely. And my return is accompanied by endless sighs.

Yes, three years, very short, but not only I have changed, even the face of my hometown has become so desolate.

Thinking that my hometown could finally let this tired returning bird rest, but the whole situation is like this, my breathing becomes more and more rapid, I can only flap my weak wings and fly out again!

Song Introduction

Village Girls

Village girls, plainly dressed, in groups of three or five, busy picking tea in the mountains. Before Grain Rain, the green tea is fragrant, the tea petals are tender green and the tea buds are yellow. Fragrant sweat flows, mouths are dry and parched, to relieve thirst and hunger, how can they bear to taste it first. Working hard, accumulating little by little, the petals are transported to the market.

Village girls, go together, sisters, busy picking mulberry leaves in the garden. The silkworms are fat, the silkworms are strong, the silkworm bodies are healthy and the silk is lustrous. Woven into satin, woven into cloth, in the cold winter and hot summer, they never try on new clothes themselves. Diligent and thrifty, accumulating inches into bolts, each piece is transported to the market. Village girls, tell their heartfelt words, busy, toiling in sericulture. Listen, the cuckoo bird, tells them that the wheat is yellow. Bitter and bitter, busy and busy, plowing and sowing, and busy with transplanting seedlings. Cautiously, not afraid of hardship, hoping for a bountiful harvest in the future. Village girls, tell their heartfelt words, hurriedly, the weather has already cooled. Look, in the city, how many beautiful clothes and red makeup. Young masters, young men, tea buds quench their thirst, jade bodies are covered in silk garments. Comfortably, warmly dressed and well fed, living in high-rise buildings with plenty of scenery.

Ballad Singing

Xia Hesheng's Three Smiles

Dunben (800) 7:00 PM to 8:00 PM

Opening "Lin Daiyu"

The beautiful and unparalleled Xiaoxiang concubine. Listening to the parrot recite poetry, my heart wants to break. The golden wind blows down the autumn parasol leaves. Her thin and delicate body feels the chill of evening. Stop embroidering. Close the gauze window. After bathing, she tidies her remaining makeup in the boudoir. Lightly applies screw shell black to paint the green of spring mountains. Lightly applies rouge and musk fragrance. With jade hairpins, she loosely combs her greasy cloud-like hair. Sheds her red shirt, revealing fragrant skin. Standing silently on the jade steps. Lightly holds a fan against the setting sun. The golden crow gradually sinks in the western mountains. The moon rises over the tips of flowers, reflecting the silver wall. Turning and twisting, she pities her beautiful shadow. Softly calls for Snow Goose to light the silver lamp. Ziju, the maidservant, asks the young lady. Why do you often sigh and weep? Her heart is full of secrets that no one understands. That's why she's so thin and her beauty fades. Helplessly, the water clock drips slowly. Loosely takes off her silk robe and goes to bed. Hears the rain hitting the banana leaves and wetting the crabapple blossoms.

Lecturing on anatomy and perspective in Chinese and Western painting lectures on wireless radio (2). On the same day, Li Shutang (940) gave a lecture on children's art education and painting in the children's program.

Afternotes

The organizer of the Shanghai Yanyan Society is Miss Ma Li's fiancé. When the Shanghai Yanyan Society broadcasts on the mainland, the two of them always go in and out together, very affectionate.

It is rumored that Yang Ping has left the Shanghai Yanyan Society and formed another ×× Society, which will begin broadcasting on XHHS soon. Is this true? (Above by Xiao Si)

Miss Zhang Suzhi, the director of the Mingmei Troupe, went to Ningbo with the Peilei Dance Troupe on October 31 to perform. It is reported that the violinist Zhang Yingjun was also with them, and they will return to Shanghai in a few days.

The Qingxin Nightingale Art Society has now stopped broadcasting. Miss Liying always likes to rush to report for others, but she never sees it through.

Miss Wenxian of the Greater Shanghai Society made six or seven phone calls one evening around 10 p.m.

Miss Liu Ling said, "When I see people playing football, I'm really a little scared, so I always lower my head and avoid them from a distance."

Miss Yang Chunmei has received almost a letter every day these past few days. (Above by Meng Ying)

Movies

"Beauty's Heart" Opens in Paris

The Xiafei Road Paris Theater will premiere the martial arts star Fan Pengke's "Beauty's Heart" today. The film tells the story of an eccentric in 19th-century Spain named "Don Juan" who loves women and chases after butterflies. Young girls and middle-aged women are all fascinated by him. This romantic affair is still widely discussed today. The props in the film imitate Spanish colors and are worth seeing.

"All-Star Gala" at the Great Light

The long-awaited Paramount musical blockbuster "All-Star Gala" (The Big Broadcast of 1936) premiered at the Great Light yesterday. It is said that the funds Paramount spent on producing this film are enough to produce ten more blockbusters, which shows its greatness. In terms of talent, not only did all of the company's musical stars and comedy stars join in, but also many stars from the American music and broadcasting industries were recruited. The producers also gathered musical styles from all over the world for the production of this film. As a result, new types of musicals are abundant, beauties of the era are as numerous as the sands of the Ganges, unique jokes emerge one after another, and exquisite backgrounds are dazzling. Everything is unprecedented, and everything is original. Among them, there is a scene of elephants dancing, which is especially amazing. These giant elephants were collected from circuses and had already received considerable training. Then, they were taught various dance styles in various ways. Their performance on stage with the dance troupe can be described as lifelike, which is truly commendable.

Silver Jottings

— Zhi Er

Gogol's "The Government Inspector" caused a sensation when it was performed by amateur actors at the Jincheng Grand Theater the other day; it is now reported that Mr. Klovsky has adapted it into a movie script, which will be produced by the Soviet Ukrainian Film Company starting this spring.

After Mr. Klovsky's adaptation, in addition to the difference in time when performing (the original play took three and a half hours to perform, and the amateur actors in Shanghai even performed it for four hours, while the adaptation into a movie is scheduled to only take eighty minutes), the scenes and actions that could not be expressed on the stage have also been added, and a critical and analytical spirit has also been added to the era when "The Government Inspector" was produced.

It is said that after Tolstoy's famous work "Resurrection" was adapted into a stage play by Donner, the Dentong colleagues will start rehearsing it from today.

It is said that Yihua Company spent hundreds of thousands of dollars, but unfortunately it has come to a miserable situation now because it was too suspicious of employing people. Today they listen to what A says, and tomorrow they change their minds and listen to what B says. As a result, the company's colleagues all have the mentality of "five days as the capital magistrate" and live a life of eating tofu, because they can't get anything else to eat.

"School for Wives" to be Staged

Ding Wanlaitian, the director of the Oriental Theater Company, and Jinshan, since they jointly performed Gogol's "The Government Inspector" with amateur actors and won general acclaim, are now directing the members of the Oriental Theater Company to rehearse Molière's famous work "School for Wives." These past few days, they have been assigning actors and urging them to familiarize themselves with the script. They will start rehearsing immediately, and they plan to rehearse it to maturity in a month. With Ding Wanlaitian's directing experience and Jinshan's acting achievements, this time directing "School for Wives" will definitely be a success. Around the tenth of next month, we can enjoy this perfect play again.

The balloon dance accompaniment in "All-Star Spotlight" is the most famous women's music team.
